Current Commentary

Tenth Anniversary of the Death of Mr. Sun Yat-sen 21

— Commemoration

Time waits for no one. Time flies like a galloping horse seen through a crack. It has been ten years since the death of Mr. Sun Yat-sen, the leader of the Chinese Kuomintang. On this tenth anniversary of his death, as we reflect on the past and look to the future, we cannot help but feel a mixture of sorrow and fear. However, there is also something to comfort us: in general, Chinese politics has been progressing toward modernization over the past decade. The warlord conflicts are no longer seen today, and the phenomenon of feudal separatism is increasingly disappearing. Even Sichuan, which has always been known for its regional warlords, is now directly under the control of the central government. Today's politics have indeed made considerable progress compared to ten years ago.

However, in terms of the economy, China is not only facing the unrecovered territories and lurking border troubles that affect the development of the national economy, but also frequent natural disasters, the decline of the countryside, the outflow of silver, panic in the cities, and widespread unemployment. These are all crises that can trigger social unrest. Therefore, as we remember Mr. Sun Yat-sen's emphasis on the spirit of "developing people's livelihood," we cannot help but feel sorrow and fear.

Furthermore, regarding foreign policy, Mr. Sun Yat-sen once said, "The goal of the National Revolution is to seek the liberation of the nation." This statement is what the Chinese people should never forget until the nation is liberated. Regarding Pan-Asianism, Mr. Sun Yat-sen once said, "The Pan-Asianism we advocate, in short, is the comparison and conflict between Eastern and Western cultures. Eastern culture is the Way of the King, while Western culture is the Way of the Hegemon. The Way of the King emphasizes benevolence, righteousness, and morality. The Way of the Hegemon emphasizes utility, strength, and power. Benevolence, righteousness, and morality are used to influence people through justice and reason. Utility, strength, and power are used to oppress people with guns and cannons." He also said, "The goal of Pan-Asianism is to unite the nations of Asia based on benevolence, righteousness, and morality, and to restore the status of Asian nations." From this perspective, Mr. Sun Yat-sen's ideal goal was to enable all Asian nations to achieve freedom, equality, and happiness, and to use benevolence, righteousness, and morality as the means to achieve this happiness. Extending this further, his ideal of Great Unity can only be achieved through these means. If there is a Pan-Asianism that goes against these means, then that is not the Pan-Asianism advocated by Mr. Sun Yat-sen. As the saying goes, "A miss is as good as a mile." This is something that the Chinese people must deeply understand as we commemorate Mr. Sun Yat-sen today.

Today, the oppression from foreign enemies and the decline of people's livelihood are more severe than they were ten years ago when Mr. Sun Yat-sen was alive. This is an undeniable fact, and there is no need to deny it. To do our best to save the situation is the common responsibility of the Chinese people today. The way to save the situation, I believe, is to first grasp a firm belief. What is that belief? It is to thoroughly implement Mr. Sun Yat-sen's diplomatic policies in foreign affairs and to work hard on "developing people's livelihood" and "universalizing people's rights" in domestic affairs. Only then may China's future have a chance.

Chairman Lin Receives Li Liejun and Others 22

He added that he was suffering from high blood pressure and mental weakness, and planned to go to Qingdao for recuperation. Commander Shen had prepared a seaside residence for him, but the train was too bumpy, and he feared that his health would not be able to withstand it. He was currently hesitating. If he did not go to Qingdao, he would return to his hometown of Wuning in Jiangxi, where he had built a small building called "Reading Building," with a couplet he wrote himself: "Wearing simple clothes, I lie among the clouds; a thousand mountains and ten thousand clouds come into my embrace," which is a true reflection of my life. (Eleventh special dispatch)

Greek Government Troops Take the Offensive; Rebel Main Force Retreats; Fortresses Fall One After Another; Three Thousand Prisoners Taken; One Warship Surrenders 26

Athens - The government announced the battle news today, saying that the central army has occupied Selles and Temishi She, and the rebels are retreating toward the Bulgarian border. According to battle reports from Trama and Jiafuria, the rebels have withdrawn from the two cities. More than 3,000 rebel officers and soldiers have surrendered. The rebels on the destroyer Eli in Jiafuria Port have also fled. (Eleventh National Telegram)

Athens - The government army's recent offensive in Eastern Macedonia has been invincible, and the rebels have shown signs of disintegration. Serres was recovered by the government army this morning, and 3,000 enemies were captured. The area is a rebel stronghold. Once it was lost, the rebel commander was greatly shocked and fled in panic. The main force is said to be retreating eastward. The government army also recaptured the cruiser Hili, which surrendered this morning in Gavalas. This is also an important victory. According to news from Alexandria Port, a ship from Crete arrived in the port today, carrying food for the rebels, but the Egyptian authorities ordered it to leave immediately. It is believed that Admiral Kolia Taikesi, commander of the rebel warship Averof, was also on the ship, but no one boarded the ship from the shore, and no one from the shore boarded the ship. (Eleventh Reuters dispatch)

The Governor of Thessaloniki, Greece, Lalis, issued a public announcement at noon stating that the government troops are progressing very rapidly, causing the entire rebel line to be in chaos. The rebels have been completely defeated, which is only a matter of days or hours. In addition, the officers of the rebel ship "Heli" have been tied up by the sailors on board. The city government and the members of the rural government council in Thessaloniki who participated in the Venizelos faction have been suspended from their duties and investigated. Telephone traffic in Thessaloniki has been restored. (Eleventh Havas dispatch)

Athens - After being defeated by the government army, the rebel officers abandoned their subordinates and fled separately, some to Gumadobi and others to Datakaji or toward the Bulgarian border. It is reported that when the government army attacked Gavala, the rebels had already abandoned the city and fled. According to Greek officials, the rebels in Eastern Macedonia and 답腊斯 can be completely eliminated today. The surrender of the rebel cruiser Heli was due to the lack of coal. It is also reported that a mutiny has occurred on the rebel warship Arilosov, which is docked at the port of Ganya. When the government army entered Serres, the residents welcomed them on both sides of the road, shouting "Long live the government." Also, when the officers who were arrested in Thessaloniki last night on suspicion of participating in the rebellion were escorted to Athens, the crowd protested against them and tried to lynch them. The people's loyalty to the government can be seen from this. (Eleventh Havas dispatch)

Greek Government Forces Occupy a Dominant Position in the General Offensive; Rebels Retreat into the Mountains 27

Athens - After deploying troops in Eastern Macedonia last week, the government army, under the command of General Kondylis, ordered a general offensive along the entire line near Serres, where the rebel headquarters is located. At the same time, 24 aircraft, loaded with bombs, flew over the enemy line, bombed the enemy's rear positions, and strafed the enemy's trenches with machine guns at low altitude. The rebels, seeing that they were outnumbered, made a slight resistance and then retreated. The government army took advantage of the victory and pressed forward. The enemy's rearguard attempted to block the government army at the Temishi Sa Bridge with light artillery, while the main force had retreated into the mountains, defending the defensive works and trenches built by the German army during the European War. The military attachés of the British and French embassies in Athens were allowed by the Greek authorities to go to the front line to observe. General Kondylis can be said to have won a bloodless victory, but he spent a lot of bullets, because when the government army bombarded, the enemy had already retreated. Although the government has won, it is still cautious. It has recently called up the 1933 air force reserve. Prime Minister Tsaldaris expressed satisfaction with the battle. Army Vice Minister General Rodopoulos said that the government army's advance is noteworthy, but the rebels are now holding the strong defensive works built during the European War, which are in a better position and easier to resist the government army's continued attack. As the government army advanced on the Macedonian front, government aircraft bombed several rebel barracks on Crete, causing many casualties. According to government officials, the total collapse of the rebels is only a matter of days. It was recently intercepted an enemy radio message proving that Venizelos also knows that the play he is directing is coming to an end. General Plastiras is believed to be the main instigator of this incident. He departed from Cannes, France, and returned to Greece. He arrived in Milan, Italy, but was unable to continue due to traffic disruption. He reluctantly returned to Cannes. According to a public announcement issued by the government, General Kondylis reported that the government army had captured 200 enemies and seized five cannons. The positions defended by the rebels were destroyed everywhere. However, at dusk, the government army encountered strong resistance from the enemy 10 miles away from Serres. The government army will be able to enter Serres this morning, and then attack Trama and Gavala. The government army lost two dead and four wounded in the battle, while the rebels suffered many casualties. It is also reported that a Greek government aircraft bombed the rebels in the Gari and port yesterday and was shot down into the sea by a warship. All three people on board escaped injury, but were captured when they landed. The rebels claim that they suffered no casualties from the aircraft bombing. (Eleventh Reuters dispatch)

(Vienna) Newspapers here received a telegram from Athens today stating that the Greek government army and the rebels fought a bloody battle on the Struma River line on Sunday, with 4,000 dead. The artillery fire was still fierce at night. Even in Athens, rebels rose up, but fortunately they were discovered early, and 600 people were arrested in the capital on Saturday night. (Eleventh National Telegram)

The Greek Civil War and International Relations; Italian Newspapers Refuse to Sit Idly By; Turkey Recognizes the Seriousness of the Situation; Bulgaria Seals the Border 28

Milan - The famous Italian newspaper "La Stampa" today published an article discussing the Greek rebellion, saying that Italy cannot ignore the revolution initiated by former Greek Prime Minister Venizelos, because such events are enough to cause serious disputes in the Balkans. The newspaper further stated that although Italy cannot take sides, Italy is the leading authority in the Mediterranean and will naturally be directly affected by such rebellions. Moreover, the Dodecanese Islands are Italian territory, so Italy should take a calm and observant attitude toward the Greek incident. (Tenth National Telegram)

Sofia - The Bulgarian authorities have sealed the Bulgarian-Greek border. It is reported that 17 guard battalions have fled from the Greek side, including the important outpost of Kula on the Sofia-Salonica Avenue. (Eleventh Reuters dispatch)

Istanbul - Turkish newspapers strongly criticized the Greek rebel ships for interfering with Turkish merchant ships. Although the government has issued a formal declaration on this matter, it recognizes the seriousness of the situation and is closely monitoring it. (Tenth National Telegram)

Ankara - The semi-official "Ulus" newspaper commented on Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu's recent declaration, saying that it is in harmony with the declaration of Turkish Foreign Minister Rushti. We fully agree with Titulescu's hope for peace in the Balkans and happiness in Greece. If the crisis in Greece can be overcome quickly, then the friendship between the Balkan Entente countries and the purpose of the Balkan Pact will be proven once again. (Tenth Havas dispatch)

Ankara - Turkish Foreign Minister Aras issued a declaration to reporters today, strongly denying the rumors that Turkey was making military preparations, saying that they were completely unfounded. The Foreign Minister said that the Turkish government is clarifying the truth of this declaration before the League of Nations and the world. Turkey has not increased a single soldier so far. However, Turkey is determined to actively exercise the rights conferred by international treaties, but in any case, it will not take any action that would harm international peace. (Tenth National Telegram)

British House of Commons Debates National Defense Issues; Labour Party to Propose a Motion of Censure Against the Government; Prime Minister Unwell and Absent 29

(London) The House of Commons will debate national defense issues today. At that time, spokespersons from all parties will have the opportunity to criticize the recent White Paper on armaments, Foreign Secretary Simon's visit to Berlin, the estimates of expenses for the army, navy, and air force, and the government's foreign policy. The debate will begin with the Labour Party formally moving that the government's national defense policy runs counter to the spirit of establishing the League of Nations to lay the foundation for collective world peace, and endangers the hope of a successful disarmament convention, which will ultimately lead to international competition and unrest. After the Labour Party proposes a vote of censure against the government, Lord President Baldwin will rise to explain the government's position. This is highly unusual, as it is customary for the explanation to come after the opposition party has spoken out and criticized. Labour MP Attlee will speak after Baldwin, and then former Foreign Secretary Austen Chamberlain will propose an amendment to the Labour Party's motion as follows: "The House of Commons is committed to the United Kingdom's obligations as a member of the League of Nations, and is willing to achieve the limitation of armaments through international compromise, and recognizes that this goal cannot be achieved by unilateral disarmament. It now agrees that the government's policy is equally necessary to protect the people and fulfill international obligations." Afterwards, Samuel Churchill and former Navy Minister Amery will speak in turn. Then Cripps will speak on behalf of the opposition party and Simon will speak on behalf of the government to conclude the debate. The opposition party, composed of the Labour Party and the Liberal Party, sees the increase of £10.5 million in defense spending as a trump card in their elections. In addition to the House of Commons debate, a large prayer meeting for peace will be held at the Victoria Street Christian Church today. After the prayer, the congregation will march to Parliament in a procession. (Eleventh Reuters dispatch)

(London) British Prime Minister MacDonald has been suffering from a cold for the past few days and is still in bed awaiting examination by a doctor. Although he can still handle important documents as usual, the doctor does not allow him to go out, so he cannot attend the House of Commons today to participate in the national defense debate. (Eleventh Reuters dispatch)

French Government Considers Extending Military Service; Three Measures Proposed; Army Reorganizes 30

(Paris) Due to the low birth rate in France during the Great War, the number of new recruits joining the army will decrease sharply from this year to 1939. In order to compensate for this shortcoming, the government plans to gradually increase the length of military service. Under the French military service system, all men are required to join the army for one year of military service at the age of 20. It is now planned to extend this to two years. The measures will be discussed at the cabinet meeting this Tuesday. According to "Le Temps," the government has proposed three measures to extend the length of military service: (1) From 1936 to 1940, the Minister of the Army shall be allowed to reduce the age of military service at his discretion, up to a limit of one year (i.e., the age of military service has always been set at 20, but it can now be reduced to 19). Within this limit, the Minister of the Army may decide to select a portion of the conscripts and order them to join the army for service; (2) The government may order the new recruits who joined the army in April 1935 to extend their military service by six months (i.e., until October 1936). From October 1935 to October 1939, new recruits will extend their military service by one year. At the same time, the number of soldiers and officers in the professional army can be increased; (3) The Minister of the Army shall be allowed to increase the army's troop strength and change the army's organization within the legal limits of the army's strength. (Tenth Havas dispatch)

Content of the Central European Pact; France Responds to German Inquiries 31

(Paris) In January, the German government said that it would like to receive more detailed information from the French government on the Central European Non-Interference Pact proposed by France and Italy. The French government has now submitted a reply to the German Embassy, ​​and the matter has progressed further. The contents of the reply have not yet been made public. According to reports, the main points of the proposed Central European Pact are as follows: (1) The former neighboring countries of Austria-Hungary and the new countries established in their territories will conclude a pact on borders and non-interference; (2) France and Italy will conclude a consultation protocol, stipulating that they should consult with each other in the event that Austria's independence is threatened; (3) Germany, Hungary, Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, Poland, and Romania should be invited to join the pact. (Tenth Reuters dispatch)

French Prime Minister Speaks on Finance and Diplomacy; France and Belgium Decide to Cooperate in Maintaining the Gold Standard; European Peace Depends on Germany's Good Will 32

Lyon - French Prime Minister Flandin said in a speech here today that the French government is making every effort to stabilize the world's major currencies, and that this is necessary to restore world prosperity. France and Belgium are now cooperating to maintain the gold standard, pending the convening of an international conference to resolve all financial issues. He also said that European peace depends on Germany's goodwill. If Germany expresses its goodwill based on equal status, permanent world peace can be expected. However, at this time, France still maintains its national defense strength. (Tenth National Telegram)

Lyon - French Prime Minister Flandin declared here today that the French government's goal is to avoid all forces that could promote the devaluation of foreign currencies, so as not to disrupt French exports. The French government cannot control the monetary policies of other countries, but French policy can prevent the influx of foreign capital. The plan recently adopted by the Bank of France, which seeks to create a short-term debt market to mitigate the dangers of contraction or devaluation, is absurdly referred to by critics as an inflationary move, because the Bank of France's cash reserves are sufficient to guarantee the current amount of banknotes issued, even if doubled. (Tenth Havas dispatch)

Lyon - Prime Minister Flandin held the opening ceremony of the Lyon Commercial Exhibition here today and was invited to a banquet by the Lyon City Government. He gave a speech on the spot, of which the section on financial policy has been seen in yesterday's telegram. The following is a continuation of the section on foreign policy, the general gist of which is as follows: Flandin said, "France is fulfilling its mission of peace in Europe. France advocates the signing of the Eastern European Pact and the Danube River Pact. Its purpose is to build a strong and unbreakable international connection to avoid any aggression. I would like to see the emerging youth forces of Europe, such as Italy and Russia, combine their spiritual forces to jointly safeguard peace. As for the Little Entente and the Balkan Entente, they have also been integrated into one body, working together within the framework of the League of Nations to prevent war. In the future, what European peace expects is Germany's good will." (Tenth Havas dispatch)

Cuba酝酿二次革命 总罢工开始京城一夜恐怖 马狄泰总统实行狄克推多 33

哈伐那 古巴共和国今日正式向总罢工各势力宣战、内阁举行特别会议后、即颁发政令、宣布全国为战时状态、并以军事法庭代普通法庭、马狄泰总统允处暴动及投掷炸弹者以死刑、昨晚总统颁布紧急状态后、事实上已成为古巴之狄克推多、但此次宣战益增总统及军人之治权、观察者称、古巴革命一触即发、双方感情激昂、一般人咸认大部份人民同情于罢工，反对军人统治、此项罢工运动为学生及教员所主动、政府之宣战未能使局势平静，政府认各处暴动系罢工工人所主持、但罢工领袖则否认此说、谓系激烈份子与失意政客所指使、罢工领袖主张向政府和平抗议、但热血之古巴人不甘软弱、人民之死于巷战及炸弹者甚多、哈伐那警察总监亦罹于难、全岛铁路已入混战状态、码头积货如山、船只停滞不能出口、美国仍抱不干涉政策、惟悉心从事护侨，闻最近暴动中有人向美国领事馆投掷砖石、如罢工工人以为美国将援助政府、则彼等或将向美侨有不利之行动也、（十一日国民电）

Accidental Fire in a Small Building at Jurentang 68

(Beiping) At 3:00 PM on the eleventh, a small building west of Jurentang in Zhongnanhai caught fire due to a sudden short circuit in the electrical wiring, which ignited the ceiling. After being extinguished by various fire brigades, the fire was completely extinguished in about ten minutes. Since no one lived there and it was used to store miscellaneous items, there was no loss. (Eleventh Day Central News Agency Dispatch)

Reorganization of Old Capital Cultural Relics Halted Due to Lack of Funds 69

(Beiping) The Old Capital Cultural Relics Reorganization Implementation Office has not made any concrete progress on various projects due to insufficient funding. In addition to the 30,000 yuan remitted by the Ministry of Finance a few days ago, the Ministry of Railways also remitted 30,000 yuan on the eleventh, both of which are temporarily deposited in the bank. The loan from the banking sector has not yet been negotiated. (Eleventh Day Central News Agency Dispatch)

A Romantic Wedding of an Old Couple 72

The groom is 88 years old, and the bride is 77 years old

(Tianjin) Zhuang Nongmin Wang Dekuan, a talented man from Jifengrun, Hebei, is 88 years old and has been a widower for a long time. Recently, through an introduction, he remarried Gao Li, a widow from Wanglipu Village, who is 77 years old, as his second wife. Gao Li has been a widow for twenty-one years. When she married, she brought a coffin for her old age as a dowry. Onlookers crowded the streets. The day after the wedding, Wang lay on his side in the bride's arms in front of his children and grandchildren, asking her to comb and braid his hair. The old woman was still too shy and gently slapped Wang's cheek with her palm. (Eleventh Day Special Dispatch)

Mei Lanfang and His Entourage Arrive in Moscow 73

(Moscow) The Soviet Union's Society for Cultural Relations with Foreign Countries has established a reception committee especially for the Chinese Mei Lanfang Troupe. Mei and others will arrive in Moscow tomorrow (the eleventh). The chairman of the committee is Alosiv, chairman of the Society for Cultural Relations with Foreign Countries. The committee members include Yan Huiqing, the Chinese ambassador to the Soviet Union, the famous stage directors Stanislavski, Dagko, Meyerhold, Tairov, the director of the Amusement Bureau, Jianiegancha, the film director Eisenstein, and the Soviet writer Tretyakov, among others. (Tenth Day TASS Dispatch)

Chen Baochen's Family Holds Public Memorial Service 82

(Fuzhou) Chen Baochen died of illness in Beiping. His clan in Gongluojiang set up a memorial service on the eleventh. Sa Zhenbing, Lin Zhiyuan, Chen Kun, and many of Chen's old friends went to Gongluo to pay their respects. (Eleventh Day Central News Agency Dispatch)

Common Shortcomings of Most County Magistrates in Zhejiang 83

(Hangzhou) Chairman Huang reported at the Provincial Government's Memorial Week on the eleventh that the common shortcomings of most county magistrates in Zhejiang Province are: (1) lack of group training, resulting in no upward progress in academic undertakings; (2) lack of creative utilization methods; (3) lack of the spirit of shifting customs, political and educational implementation, and only focusing on tangible political orders; (4) uncleanliness of government offices; (5) inability to supervise and report subordinates; (6) excuse of lack of money, resulting in perfunctory and decadent phenomena; (7) excuse of lack of power and ignorance of establishing authority; (8) inability to thoroughly understand various problems in the county; (9) misunderstanding of the intentions of superiors and the talent and integrity of subordinates. In order to remedy the above problems, it was decided to convene a training session for all county magistrates in the province next month in order to achieve practical administrative results. He also said that the current three-month design period has expired, the policy plan has been largely determined, and the next three months will be the preparation period so that new policies can begin to be implemented starting next year. (Eleventh Day Central News Agency Dispatch)

Japanese Intensify Oppression of Chinese in Northeast; Chinese Must Hang Japanese Flags on Japanese Memorial Days; Disobedience is Deemed Anti-Japanese and Counterfeit 84

Dalian Dispatch: The Pan-Asian Society, presided over by Japanese national Okawa Shumei, recently held a general meeting of all its cadres and decided to intensify the oppression of Chinese people within the Kwantung Leased Territory. The resolutions are as follows: (1) On the four major festivals and other Japanese memorial days, Chinese people in the Kwantung Leased Territory must hang Japanese flags on every household to show respect; (2) The population of Chinese people in the territory should be specially investigated, and no people of different surnames should be allowed to reside there; (3) Crimes committed by Chinese people in the territory should be severely punished, without a trial system, but instead with an immediate decision system; (4) Manchurian officials who remit funds from the territory to China, or deposit funds in Chinese banks, are subject to strict restrictions. In order to effectively implement the resolutions, the Society jointly monitors the compliance of Chinese people in the territory with the Asia Youth League on the one hand, and on the other hand, Okawa Shumei leads three cadres to visit Kobayashi Tei and another assistant officer of the Dalian Branch of the Fengtian Special Service Agency, and the police authorities, requesting joint suppression. All are said to have been agreed upon and will be implemented on February 11, Foundation Day. Chinese people who do not comply will be charged with anti-Manchu and anti-Japanese crimes. According to them, this measure is to impose collective punishment on non-pro-Japanese elements and even anti-Japanese and anti-Manchu elements. In fact, it forces Chinese people to recognize themselves as "Manchukuo" people and obey the orders of the Japanese. (Northeast News Agency)

Situation of the Yutian Security Team Transferring Defense as Ordered 85

Beiping Dispatch: The Yutian War Zone Security Supplementary Brigade has been ordered to transfer defense. The special team of the Supplementary Brigade, led by Feng Shoupeng, consisting of 602 men, and Sun Jizhou, the former acting commander, set off on foot from Yutian to Tangshan at 6:00 AM on the eighth, arriving around 2:00 PM. The supplies, weapons, ammunition, and horses had set off earlier on the seventh. The remaining three units of Sun Yuchen, Wang Zixiu, and Liu Benzhi left Yutian on the ninth, passing through Ji County, Sanhe, and heading to Xiazhen and Yanjiao. The Commissioner of the Jiji-Miyun District, Yin Rugeng, ordered them to set off immediately, and they obeyed and left the territory. The two new security teams of Zhang Yantian and Zhang Jingyu were originally scheduled to enter the war zone after Chairman Yu Xuezhong of Hebei Province returned to Tianjin. Recently, the two Commissioners of Jiji-Miyun-Luan-Yu received a telegram from Yu, ordering them to change defenses immediately. Therefore, it has been decided that after the transfer of defense of the Yutian Security Team is completed, they will separately enter the Luan-Yu and Jiji-Miyun districts to take over the defense.

After the war zone security team changes defense, the distribution of its new defense areas has been announced by the Jiji-Miyun District Commissioner's Office as follows: The First Brigade of the Hebei Province War Zone Security Team will be stationed in the Pingxi Tongzhou Huairou area; the Second Brigade, led by Zhou Yuying, will be stationed in Yutian County; the Third Brigade, led by Yang Yucheng, will be stationed in Changli, Lulong and other counties; the newly entered Fourth Brigade, led by Zhang Yantian, will be stationed in Funing County, Qinhuangdao, Haiyangzhen, and other areas; another newly entered brigade will be stationed in Pingxi; the First Brigade of the War Zone Security Team, led by Liu Zuozhou, will be stationed in Luan County; the Second Brigade, led by Zhao Lei, will be stationed in Funing County and Tangshan. The special team of the supplementary brigade, led by Feng Shoupeng, is under the command of Zhao Lei and is stationed in Tangshan. Li Yunsheng's unit is stationed between Tongzhou and Sanhe. The Hebei Provincial Security Team has a total of 12,000 men, the War Zone Security Team has 5,000 men, and the special police force has 1,300 men. (Ninth Day)

Anti-Banditry Arrangement in the Border Area of Zhejiang, Fujian and Jiangxi Provinces - Liu Heding and Chen Shizheng are Appointed as Commanders Respectively 86

Fuzhou Dispatch: Since the annihilation of the two bandit forces of Fang Zhimin and Peng Dehuai on the border of Zhejiang, Fujian and Jiangxi provinces, there have been no large bandit forces, but scattered bandits are still rampaging. Now, Liu Heding, stationed in Jian'ou by the Military Commission, and Chen Shizheng, stationed in Longquan, are the commanders and deputy commanders for anti-banditry in the border area of Zhejiang, Fujian and Jiangxi provinces. The nine counties of Songxi, Zhenghe, Pucheng, Chong'an, Longquan, Qingyuan, Taishun, Jiangshan, and Changshan are designated as the areas for suppression. All the troops and militia in these nine counties are under their unified command. Liu and Chen have already taken office in their respective defense areas. Since the areas of Shanghai, Xiamei in the second region of Chong'an, Xingcun, Liyuan, Chenghu in the fifth region, and Yangzhuang, Sidu, Huangshi, and Da'an in the seventh region have been recovered one after another by the garrison troops during the year, the aftermath of the recovered bandit areas was reported to the province yesterday by Huang Xiangchen, the county magistrate. After receiving the report, the provincial government reviewed and instructed the tenth district administrative commissioner to comply with the following: (1) It is said that the returning people are in extreme suffering. It has been negotiated with the Provincial Disaster Relief Association to borrow 2,000 yuan, which will be specially lent to farmers and must be repaid within five months by the county magistrate; (2) It is said that the baojia system in districts 1, 4, and 6 has been completed in order, except that districts 2 and 7 have not yet been recovered, and districts 3, 5, 8, and 9 are all obedient and progressing. Efforts are still being made to supervise and promote the system to complete self-defense as soon as possible. In addition, the principles for handling the aftermath in Changting have also been meticulously planned by the responsible authorities of the province and have been determined. The provincial government has ordered the administrative commissioner of the eighth district to follow them: (1) The establishment of a farmers' loan office will be supervised and carried out by personnel sent by the Disaster Relief Association. If necessary, personnel will be sent by the Rural Financial Relief Office to guide it. The recovered loans will still be retained locally to continue to handle rural lending affairs; (2) The establishment of weaving and paper mills will be the responsibility of Lin Sixian to select personnel. The Construction Department will send personnel to inspect and supervise the progress at any time. The purpose of all paper mill profits is to maintain the local paper industry as much as possible; (3) One0,000 yuan for disaster relief from the Nanchang Headquarters and one0,000 yuan for disaster relief allocated by this province will be handed over to the Disaster Relief Association to establish a farmers' loan office in Ting, the distribution of which is as follows: (A) 3,500 yuan for urgent relief; (B) 8,500 yuan for agricultural relief; (C) 8,000 yuan for weaving mills. In addition, to engage in the paper-making business, the funds will be borrowed by the Disaster Relief Association for 5,000 yuan and by the Construction Department for 5,000 yuan, and will be repaid by the paper mill within six months; (4) The implementation of the work section should be postponed, and the commissioner Lin will execute it. The progress will be announced to local groups at any time, and there is no need to set up a separate industrial society to save procedures. (March 9)

Founding of Jiangxi Provincial Federation of Commerce - More Than 100 Proposals Resolved at the Representatives Conference 87

Nanchang Dispatch: The Jiangxi Provincial Chamber of Commerce Representatives Conference was held a few days ago. There were five general meetings, and more than 100 proposals from the chambers of commerce of various cities, counties, and towns were resolved. The important proposals are as follows: (1) Now that the Red bandits have been suppressed, please lift the blockade on various counties so that salt, kerosene, etc. can be freely bought and sold; (2) Abolish the post-banditry disaster relief donation; (3) Please ask the Pacification Headquarters to wipe out the scattered bandits in various places; (4) Local products have declined in various places, resulting in commercial depression, and methods should be found to develop special products to maintain commerce; (5) Establish a provincial commercial joint bank; (6) Please ask the government to exempt merchants from military service; (7) Rural areas are bankrupt due to water, drought, and banditry disasters, please ask the government to provide relief; (8) Merchants in various places should vigorously implement the New Life Movement; (9) Start a commercial daily newspaper; (10) Determine the fee grade for the provincial federation of commerce: (11) the special-grade Nanchang Municipal Chamber of Commerce will undertake 80 yuan per year; the first-grade Jiujiang, Jingdezhen, etc. chambers of commerce will undertake 60 yuan per year; the second-grade Ji'an, Ganzhou, etc. chambers of commerce will undertake 40 yuan per year; the third-grade counties and towns chambers of commerce will undertake 40 yuan per year, the third-grade is 20 yuan, and the fourth-grade is 20 yuan. The executive and supervisory committee members of the provincial federation were elected on the ninth. As a result, Xu Huaiqing, Xu Ruifu, Wan Zhucun, Chen Zhongxi, Chen Xitao, Liang Zhaonan, Liang Rendao, Lu Fang, Wang Hanzhou, Zou Rixun, Xiong Jikang, Lu Qiran, Zheng Yaoting, Gan Ruyong, etc. were elected as executive committee members; Xu Luxuan, Gong Zhipeng, Hu Bingwen, Yang Xiangfu, Ai Zhongxiang, Wen Xiangong, Yang Qinxian, and Xing Zhongquan were elected as supervisory committee members. The Provincial Federation of Commerce was established on the same day, as the highest authority of the provincial chamber of commerce. The representatives of the conference originally planned to visit the Linchuan Experimental Zone, but due to time constraints, they have returned separately. (March 9)

Closing of the Hubei Provincial Administrative Conference - 53 Cases Resolved 88

Hankou Dispatch: The Hubei Provincial Administrative Conference was officially opened on the fourth and ended on the eighth. All the proposals from various parties have been discussed and resolved a total of 53 cases, of which the civil administration and security part is the largest, followed by construction, finance, and education. On the afternoon of the eighth, the conference held a closing ceremony, and the provincial chairman Zhang Qun delivered a closing speech, which roughly stated, "Since the closing of this conference, it has been five days. More than 50 important cases have been resolved. Whether in the plenary meeting or in the group review, colleagues have been able to carefully discuss each issue and reach a compromise. It is sufficient to show the colleagues' spirit and concentration and emotional tension. Although the meeting time is short, the results are quite satisfactory. It is gratifying that today's meeting opened as scheduled. During the meeting, we thank the heads of various agencies for their guidance and encouragement, and at the same time, the expectations of public opinion have given colleagues great encouragement. This is also what colleagues deeply feel grateful for. Looking at all 53 cases of this conference, according to the administrative nature, the civil affairs part is the most, with a total of 14 cases, 13 cases in the security part, 12 cases in the construction part, 7 cases in the financial part, and 6 cases in the education part. In addition to the proposals from the government, the commissioners proposed a total of 14 cases, and added 7 opinions for the reference of the meeting. On the day the conference opened, I mentioned the main purpose of convening this conference and the four meanings it contains, namely, governance, management, cultivating people's power, and using land. In terms of various resolutions, there are many that cultivate people's power, totaling 26 cases, accounting for almost one-half of the total. People's power can be divided into morality, knowledge, organization, and production, four kinds of power. Among these 26 cases, there are 10 cases on increasing the people's productivity. This is enough to show that colleagues are concerned about the people's livelihood and are willing to work hard, but when it comes to local construction and facilities, there is still a feeling of being overwhelmed by details. For the purpose of simplifying administration and managing complexity, we should pay close attention to the following points: (1) Respect laws and regulations; (2) Improve the system; (3) Prepare budgets; (4) Develop education; (5) Vigorously implement production construction; (6) Consolidate finances. The conference was held during the beautiful spring season when plants are sprouting. The ancients said, "A day's plan lies in the morning, and a year's plan lies in the spring." Therefore, the result of this conference is the entire plan for the policy implementation in the coming year. Each commissioner will implement it earnestly after returning to the district, which is needless to say. Although this year is the first provincial administrative conference, it will be a precedent next year. In the future, it will be convened once a year, and when it is convened again next year, we must first check the work in this year, whether our efforts are sufficient, and whether all policies are thoroughly implemented. This will be the test. This is what I would like to encourage colleagues to do together." After the closing of the conference, Zhang summoned the heads of various departments and administrative commissioners once again to discuss it, as he had received a winter telegram from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, and the heads of various departments and commissioners should go to Jiangxi and Guangdong to investigate construction, baojia education, etc. It was decided that they would set off in turn, and the first batch would start within this month.

Songjiang, Sijing Town Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs Request for Exemption from Increased House Tax 90

Since this month, Jiangsu Province has generally levied house tax in various counties. The revised new regulations have not only not gone through legal procedures, but also have excessively heavy tax rates, which the people cannot afford. The Sijing Town Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram on behalf of the province's finance department yesterday, requesting that the old regulations be restored. The original telegram said, "To Director Zhao of the Finance Department of Jiangsu Province: It is reported that the house tax in various counties of this province will be levied on March 1 this year, regardless of self-produced rented houses, shops and residents, all need to be generally collected, and the shops will be taxed at 15 percent, and residents will pay 8 percent per month. To increase or decrease the rate, the county shall follow the provisions of Articles 3, 4 and 7 of the Central Supervision of Local Finance Provisional Regulations. There are clear provisions, and this sudden increase comes at a time when industry and commerce are declining and the rural economy is bankrupt. The original shops are closing down one after another, and there are many empty houses on the market. How can there be any surplus capacity to increase the burden? For this reason, we urge the Director to withdraw the order and keep the house tax in the various counties as it was, so as to relieve the people of Jiangsu and emphasize the rule of law. The Songjiang County Sijing Town Chamber of Commerce, Chairman Li Xiuze, signature."

A Record of Re-Visiting Pan Pool and Paying Respect to the Sage 91

Zhu Yunxin, styled Sishi, a respected elder of this county, aged 73, was a successful candidate in the imperial examination in the late Qing Dynasty, and served as the president of the Zhejiang Provincial Trial Court and as a bureaucrat in the central government. Ye Tiwen, from Shanghai, aged 78, was a successful candidate in the provincial examination in the late Qing Dynasty, and served as the principal of the Provincial Third Middle School, Shanghai Jingye School and Tsinghua University in Beijing. This year marks the 60th anniversary of their successful examination, and they hold a ceremony of re-visiting Pan Pool and paying respects to the sage according to custom. Today (11th), Zhu and Ye jointly held the ceremony, wearing blue shirts and peacock feather hats, hiring the ceremonial guards who welcomed the successful candidates in the former Qing Dynasty, and parading through the city in an orderly manner to the Confucius Temple to worship the Most Holy Teacher, performing the rituals respectfully. Many people from all walks of life went to congratulate them. This event is a relic from 30 years ago, so those who went to the Confucius Temple to watch the ceremony filled the streets.

Silkworm Improvement Expert Dr. Mary Injured in Car Accident

Near Zhapu on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway

Ni Zhaotai Suffers Two Broken Elbow Bones

According to the Guowen News Agency, Dr. Mary, an Italian expert from the National Economic Commission's Silkworm Improvement Committee, was ordered by the Nanjing Experimental Department of the committee on the morning of the 8th to go to Zhejiang to inspect the condition of silkworms. She immediately set off with her daughter, clerk Ni Zhaotai, and driver Qiu, a total of four people, in a black-plated car with Shanghai license plate number 5386, heading to Hangzhou along the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway. At about 3:00 PM that day, when passing the Lujiaqiao area near Zhapu, there were two elderly women walking in the middle of the road. The driver suddenly saw people walking in front of the car and swerved sharply to the left. Unexpectedly, in a hurry, the car crashed violently into the stone railing next to the bridge, causing the occupants to be injured. Except for Ms. Mary's beloved daughter, who was unharmed, Ms. Mary herself broke her right arm bone, clerk Ni Zhaotai broke his head and fractured two elbow bones, and driver Qiu was injured in the head. Villagers discovered the accident and carried the injured to Zhapu Chengji Hospital. The Lujiaqiao Public Security Bureau directly telegraphed the Shanghai Silkworm Improvement Association. Upon hearing the news, committee member Guo Dehua immediately dispatched a car to rescue them. That night, the injured were sent to Shanghai. Ms. Mary was sent to the Public Concession Hospital, and Ni and the driver Qiu were sent to the Tongren Hospital for treatment. Yesterday, reporters inquired at various hospitals and learned that Ms. Mary's right arm was broken, and the bone had been fractured. After surgery, her condition was good. Ni broke his head and fractured two elbow bones, one of which was broken into three pieces, so his injuries were the most serious. Driver Qiu's head was also injured by the car's front glass, and his condition was not light. He also suffered chest injuries and was spitting blood. All were bandaged and treated by the hospital. It is said that it will take several months of treatment before they can be discharged.

Industrial and Commercial Decline Leads to Increased Unemployment

The Municipal Federation of Trade Unions Requests Relief

And Issues a Letter to All Workers in the City

Advising to Work Hard and Intensify Production

According to the Dagong News Agency, due to the sluggish market, industrial and commercial decline, and the sharp increase in the number of unemployed workers, the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions yesterday submitted a special request to the central ministries and commissions, requesting them to quickly determine effective measures and implement relief, and issued a letter to all workers in the city, advising them to work hard and intensify production, and not to strike or slack off unless absolutely necessary, in order to maintain industrial development. The telegrams are excerpted below:

Requesting Central Government to Grant Relief Swiftly

To the Executive Committee of the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, and the Ministry of Finance: Since the outbreak of the world economic panic in 1929, all countries have been implementing economic blockade policies in order to seek self-help. In addition to building high tariff barriers to prevent the intrusion of foreign goods, they have also implemented dumping of surplus goods in China. Our country's budding industry and commerce have suffered a severe blow, leading to a sharp decline in exports and the brink of extinction of foreign sales. The serious situation is an undeniable fact. If we do not quickly seek relief and devise countermeasures, the consequences will be unpredictable. The association witnessed the precarious situation and could not remain silent. In addition to advising all workers in the city to share the difficulties, adhere to the principle of shared prosperity and adversity, and work hard to intensify production with a spirit of perseverance, we implore your committees (yuan and ministries) to strictly order manufacturers in all industries to take the overall situation into consideration, endure the pain and barely maintain the current situation, and not to rashly suspend operations or lay off workers, so as to reduce unemployment and maintain social order. At the same time, we should properly devise effective measures to implement relief and quickly decide on the overall economic policy for the future, in order to stabilize finance and industry prospects. The safety of the nation depends on this. The telegram is sent with utmost urgency.

Advising Workers to Intensify Production

The association yesterday issued a letter to all workers in the city, saying: Dear workers of the city, since the January 28th Incident, industry and commerce in our city have been declining, and vitality has not been restored. Coupled with the wave of the world economic panic and the deep bankruptcy of domestic rural areas, all industries have fallen into a state of extreme decline. After the end of the major strike, the instability of finance has further aggravated the difficulties and critical situation of industry and commerce. Under such a serious situation, labor and capital are facing unprecedented difficulties, both being exploited by international capitalism. In order to get rid of the current difficulties and seek the survival of the entire nation, we must be of one mind and cooperate sincerely, adhering to the principle of shared prosperity and adversity, and work hard to intensify production with a spirit of perseverance. Unless absolutely necessary, we cannot strike or slack off at will, so as to prevent the already precarious industry and commerce from suffering any further blows. We can only align our steps, work hard, resist the economic oppression of various imperialist powers, and promote the development of national industry. Only then can our personal lives be improved, and the entire nation have a way out. Respectfully announced by the Shanghai Municipal Federation of Trade Unions.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Expands Coastal and Inland River Shipping

Purchase of American Sea Vessels... Construction of River Vessels

The purchase of sea vessels from the American Shipping Department by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company was initially introduced by Ralph W. Weymoath. Later, after negotiations with the American Shipping Department by our country's consul in Seattle, the matter was changed to direct consultation between our Ministry of Finance and the US government. The Ministry of Finance requested the blueprints of the sea vessels to be sold by the American Shipping Department be sent first for selection. On January 20th of this year, the American Shipping Department sent the blueprints of more than 300 sea vessels for sale, except for those marked with red lines, completely to the Ministry of Finance for submission to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company for purchase.

Vessels Selected

The company received Ministry Order No. 1363 and blueprints of various ships. After repeated consideration by the director of the shipbuilding department and the chief shipowner, it was decided to select twelve sea vessels and three iron barges with a draft and tonnage suitable for navigation along the coasts of North and South China. The carrying capacity of the sea vessels ranges from 3,000 to 5,000 tons, while the iron barges are 500 tons. After the selection, the remaining ship samples were sent back, and a report was submitted to the Ministry of Finance, requesting negotiations with the US government regarding the purchase price.

Negotiations in Progress

Our Ministry of Finance is conducting negotiations with the representative of the American Shipping Department's Shanghai office. Meanwhile, a special commissioner has been dispatched to inspect the hulls of the ships. These procedures are currently in progress. After the ship prices are negotiated, the Ministry of Finance will pay on behalf of the company and transfer the funds to the company's capital account in the future, so the company will not need to spend huge sums.

Construction of River Vessels

The purchase of twelve American sea vessels has become a reality. The development of Yangtze River steamships has also been decided to be expedited simultaneously. Using a portion of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity, more than 50,000 pounds, it was originally planned to build one large Yangtze River vessel and two shallow-water river vessels for the upper reaches. The matter was submitted to the board of directors last week. After discussion, it was decided to temporarily suspend the shallow-water river vessel plan and focus on building two Yangtze River steamships, each with a tonnage of over 3,000 tons. All raw materials for one vessel will be purchased from the UK, and the rest will be built in the country. The new shipbuilding committee has been ordered to quickly draft blueprints, aiming to finalize the bidding and construction in the shortest possible time.

Li Jingcong Discusses Negotiation Situation

Gao Xibing to Come to Shanghai for Further Discussions

Both Parties Agree to Resume Flights

Overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia Request Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to

Only Allow Chinese Ships to Sail to Southeast Asia

Can Reduce Freight Costs on National Goods

Making Sales in Southeast Asia Easier

According to the Central News Agency, according to news from overseas Chinese affairs organizations in this port, the overseas Chinese living in Southeast Asia have been subjected to various oppressions in recent years, causing their businesses to decline day by day. The sales of domestic goods to Southeast Asia have also decreased as a result. Although there are many reasons for this, the fact that Chinese ships do not sail to Southeast Asia is the biggest reason. Because Chinese ships do not sail to Southeast Asia, the transportation of Chinese goods is inevitably carried out on foreign ships, resulting in unequal and exorbitant freight charges on foreign ships. The prices of goods are high, making sales difficult, and sales have decreased day by day. In view of this, the overseas Chinese have now requested the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to quickly find a cargo ship to sail to Southeast Asia, so that the transportation of domestic goods will not be subjected to such unequal treatment again.

Total Length of 2 Kilometers, Completion in July

The municipal government of this city, in view of the development of the city center relying on convenient transportation, in addition to the waterway construction of the Qiu River wharf, requested the Ministry of Railways last year to build a railway from Gaojingmiao Station on Songhu Road to in front of the municipal government. The entire project is the responsibility of the Lianglu Administration. The entire line runs from Gaojingmiao Station on Sanmin Road to the intersection of Wusong Road, with a total length of approximately 2 kilometers and an estimated cost of 45,000 yuan.

Completion in July of This Year

Since being ordered to handle the project, the Lianglu Bureau has been actively carrying it out. The earthwork project of the bureau was put out for tender last month, and four companies submitted bids: Changji, Zhenliji, Cailinji, and Yishen. Changji won the bid with the lowest price, and it has now been approved by the Ministry of Railways to officially start filling the earth today. For the bridge project, six companies submitted bids: Chalinji, Zhang Binxun, Yishen, Yang Changji, Changji, and Zhenchang. As a result, Cailinji won the bid with the lowest construction cost of 4,484 yuan. Construction will also start in the coming days. The entire project is expected to be completed and open to traffic before July of this year.

Opening Ceremony of the Public Security Bureau Police Training School Yesterday

Mayor Wu and Director Cai Delivered Speeches

According to the Central News Agency, the Municipal Public Security Bureau Police Training School has trained more than 500 police cadets in the 16th and 17th classes since its resumption in the winter of the year before last. Therefore, a supplementary opening ceremony was held yesterday (the 11th) at 10:00 AM. Mayor Wu, Director Cai, and many guests from military, political, and party organizations attended the ceremony. All police cadets were able to perform with full spirit and rapid movements. Director Cai chaired the meeting, reported on the preparation process and the general situation of the police cadets. Then, Mayor Wu Tiecheng delivered a speech, saying: When the Premier was dying, he told us to "seek peace, oppose internal strife, and save China." For the past ten years, our party has been working hard according to this saying, removing obstacles to peace, and completing the mission of securing the interior and resisting foreign aggression. The police have an extremely important responsibility in this work. The police are executing the laws for the country, so the police themselves must have a sound body and receive strict police education. Therefore, from now on, you should study the subjects well and implement a new lifestyle, starting with your own food, clothing, shelter, and transportation, so as to become good police officers in the future and serve the country and society. Director Cai then delivered a speech, saying: We must follow Mayor Wu's instructions and strive to promote a new lifestyle. But we must also know that the Premier said, "Knowing is difficult, acting is easy." We police are the nannies and teachers of the people. We must have a higher level of knowledge than the people. You police officers are now receiving training at the training school. It is the time when you should work hard to acquire knowledge. When you graduate in the future, it will be the time to act. If you do not work hard now, you will definitely not gain the trust of the people in the future, and you will definitely not be able to shoulder the responsibilities of a nanny and a teacher. You must make up your mind from now on to serve the police force of Shanghai loyally and bravely, so as to be worthy of the country and Mayor Wu's instructions. A photo was then taken to commemorate the event.

Executive Yuan Orders Protection of People's Property and Freedom of Business

Municipal Government Orders Subordinates to Comply

According to the Central News Agency, the Municipal Government of this city received an order from the Executive Yuan to protect the people's property and freedom of business, and therefore specially ordered its subordinates to comply. The original order is recorded below: "Zhaoming previously proposed to the Central Political Conference with Chairman Jiang to protect the people's property and freedom of business, which has been passed by the Central Political Conference and communicated to all subordinates of the National Government for compliance. Another detailed telegram has been sent, which I think you have noted. In order to implement this resolution, if there are any requests to seal up or confiscate the people's property, or restrict or prohibit the people's freedom of business for any reason, serious attention should be paid to them. If the request comes from the party headquarters, the provincial and municipal governments should immediately telegraph the request to the central government and wait for approval to handle it according to law. If the request comes from other organizations, the provincial and municipal governments should immediately reject it and issue a reprimand, without showing any favoritism, so as not to undermine the spirit of the rule of law and cause suffering to the people. This is of utmost importance. A special telegram is sent to you for compliance." While complying, another micro-telegram from the Executive Yuan was received, stating: "The National Government approved the letter from the Central Political Conference, stating that in accordance with Articles 16 and 37 of the Provisional Constitution, the people's property and freedom of business are protected by the Provisional Constitution. However, in recent times, local officials have often infringed upon the people's property and hindered the people's freedom of business under various pretexts, which is an undeniable violation of the law. If this is not rectified immediately, how can we maintain official integrity and uphold the rule of law? It is proposed that the National Government be notified by letter from this conference and instructed to ensure the protection of the people's life, property, and freedom of business in accordance with the rules for exercising administrative power, and not to infringe upon them arbitrarily. Is this appropriate? Please decide by public vote, etc. The resolution was passed at the 446th meeting of this conference and sent to the Standing Committee and the National Government. In addition to separate letters, the case is hereby recorded and a letter is sent for compliance and instructed for unified compliance, etc. Approved, it should be handled accordingly. In addition to responding by letter and distributing separately, this order is hereby issued for compliance and instructed for unified compliance." Following this, in addition to distributing the order separately, this order is hereby issued for your information.

Dried Cocoon Sources Cut Off

Silk Factories Close One After Another

Only Five Are Still Operating

Silk Merchants Request Assistance from the Authorities

According to the Dagong News Agency, due to the Zhejiang Provincial Government's implementation of cocoon control last year, the dried cocoons produced could not be transported and sold outside the province. The cocoons produced in the Jiangsu production areas such as Suzhou, Changzhou, Wuxi, Jin, Danyang, Yixing, and Cheng, etc., were all purchased by the silk factories in Wuxi because of their proximity, resulting in a cut-off of dried cocoon sources in Shanghai. Although cocoon merchants had stored a lot of dried cocoons last year, they were all pledged to banks, increasing costs. According to the recent overseas silk market, they still have to suffer losses, resulting in the depletion of raw materials in various factories. The eleven silk factories that started operations after the Spring Festival have successively shut down in the past two days. Currently, only five factories in the city are still struggling to operate: Rixin in the South Shanghai area, Jiyu in the Xinzao area, Meifeng, Sheng in the Hongkou area, and Fulun (Dupion). However, half of them are still processing on behalf of others. Once the remaining cocoons are reeled, they will also stop operating. According to silk industry sources who spoke to the Dagong News Agency, it is still difficult to predict whether silk merchants in Shanghai will be allowed to purchase dried cocoons when the spring cocoons come on the market this year. Therefore, the industry has requested assistance from the authorities to avert the crisis.

Appeal by Cixi Natives in Shanghai to Recover Road Shares

Mr. Yang Yisheng, a prominent financier from Cixi living in Shanghai, stated that the 300,000 yuan for the Cixi National Defense Highway was ordered by the provincial government to be collected and allocated from the county's tax and land items. Last year, Cixi suffered a severe drought, and the farmers could not bear the burden. Therefore, Mr. Yang invited fellow villagers to prepare cash to redeem the road shares to provide relief. Recently, Mr. Yang stated that the National Defense Highway in Zhejiang Province is mostly built with funds allocated by the provincial government, while Cixi's funds are collected from the people, which is unfair. Therefore, he submitted a petition to Chairman Jiang and the provincial government authorities, requesting that the road shares be purchased by the Tongyun Automobile Company and merged for handling, or that the provincial government prepare funds to recover the shares, following the example of the Zhenluo Road, to alleviate the people's difficulties. At a time when the rural areas are bankrupt and the farmers cannot afford to live from morning till night, Mr. Yang's move should be viewed optimistically by the people of the area.

Labor Nursery School to Pilot Night Care

Registration Starts Today, Limited to 15 Children, Monthly Fee 6-8 Yuan, Not Limited to Labor Children

The First Labor Nursery School, sponsored by the Municipal Children's Welfare Committee, has been providing mobile childcare for more than 30 children since its opening. It has now decided to pilot night care, and registration will start from today. The details are as follows:

Cultivating Nursery Talents

According to Hu Shuyi, Standing Committee Member of the Children's Welfare Committee, speaking to a Shanghai News Agency reporter, the Labor Nursery School sponsored by the committee is the only nursery school in the city piloting childcare. The pilot has been effective, and it will continue to be operated permanently. It is also planned to operate nursery schools in the residences of civilians in the city in the future, and a large number of childcare talents are needed. The Labor Nursery School is also the place to cultivate these talents. Daycare has been piloted for several months and has been quite successful, so it has been decided to pilot night care.

Pilot Night Care

The school will pilot night care, accepting a temporary enrollment of 15 children, not limited to labor children. The monthly fee is 6 to 8 yuan. Registration starts from today. When the pilot is effective, it will operate day and night care. At that time, in addition to those who wish to experiment, the monthly fee for labor children will still be 2 yuan.

Self-Made Scientific Soybean Milk

In order to meet the needs of the children of the working class, the school usually uses soybean milk to feed the children. Soybean milk is cheaper and more nutritious. However, purchasing it from outside is more expensive. Therefore, it uses scientific methods to make soybean milk for its own use and can also supply the needs of society. The selling price is cheap and hygienic. All sectors who wish to try it can contact the school quickly.

Zhabei Businessmen and Residents Discuss Concerns Regarding Huxiang Train's Impact on Traffic

Propose Two Remedial Measures: Constructing an Overpass and Relocating the Station

Zhabei businessmen and residents, such as the Bazhou Business Community Joint Association, etc., believe that Zhabei has a vast area and that the main roads for north-south traffic, in addition to the Baoshan Road overpass, are only Gonghexin Road and Datong Road. In the past, the Songhu train had its ticket office located next to the North Station, and the train often opened and closed the gates at Baoshan Road, which hindered traffic. After opposition from citizens, the ticket office was moved to the east side of Saisan Road, which made it more convenient for vehicles and pedestrians. Recently, the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways have had no less than 40 or 50 passenger and freight trains, pressing cars, etc., going back and forth every day. Each time they pass through the gates of Gonghexin Road and Datong Road, the gates must be closed, and traffic is often interrupted. Recently, the Huxiang double track has been laid, and the Shanghai-Nanxiang line is about to open to traffic. It is also heard that this special train has 20 round trips every day, so the opening and closing of the gates will also increase 20 times. The time for each opening and closing is calculated to be 10 minutes, so the round trip of each train will take 10 hours a day. The traffic on Gonghexin Road and Datong Road will be frequently interrupted. The loss of time suffered by businessmen and residents in their daily commutes is unimaginable. Therefore, it is learned that the businessmen and residents are now proposing two remedial measures, namely: (1) Request the authorities to build a steel and cement overpass so that vehicles and pedestrians can pass over the bridge, and the Wanfu Nunnery north of the Datong Road railway will need to be demolished because it protrudes beyond the route; (2) If the first proposal cannot be implemented, please move the Huxiang train ticket office to the Maigen Road Station on the west end of Datong Road. The above remedial measures are currently under discussion. Whether there will be any changes in the future will depend on the final decision, which will be submitted to the Ministry of Railways for approval and then forwarded to the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration for implementation.

Two-Week Anniversary of the Sun Yat-sen Cultural and Educational Center and Inauguration Ceremony of the New Building (Nanjing, 11th) The Sun Yat-sen Cultural and Educational Center will hold its two-week anniversary celebration and the inauguration ceremony of its new building at 10 a.m. on the 12th. The event will be chaired by Sun Ke, Chairman of the Center's Board of Directors, who will report on the work progress. Director Pan of the Education Bureau Discusses Education in the Philippines Elementary Education is Particularly Developed; Education is Completely Free for Students Overseas Chinese in the Philippines Recently Organized an Overseas Chinese Education Association Overseas Chinese Elementary School Students Can Understand Mandarin, Which is Not the Case Domestically Mr. Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Shanghai Education Bureau, recently returned to Shanghai after participating in a tourism group to the Philippines, where he investigated educational affairs. A reporter from the Shanghai News Agency specifically visited Mr. Pan yesterday. According to Mr. Pan, the situation of education in the Philippines is as follows: "I participated in a tourism group to the Philippines and can briefly describe the educational affairs there. During the Spanish colonial period, most schools in the Philippines were run by the Catholic Church, emphasizing religion. Churches from one or two hundred years ago can often be seen. Since the American administration, over the past 40 years, considerable effort has been put into education, so the progress of education has been very rapid. Under the Governor-General of the Philippines, there is a Department of Education, which has an Education Bureau under it. Educational funding accounts for more than 20% of the total annual expenditure of governments at all levels. The total population of the Philippines is about 12 million, and the number of students is about 1.1 million, of which elementary school students number about 1 million, accounting for about 8% of the population. The Philippine government is now working hard to promote education. Their elementary schools are completely free, so there is no need for coercive measures; people voluntarily enroll. Unfortunately, there are still not enough elementary schools, so increasing the number of schools and expanding enrollment has become an absolute necessity. All of the United States' facilities in the Philippines are not intended for permanent occupation of the land, but rather to cultivate the Filipinos and improve their knowledge and abilities day by day so that they can govern themselves and achieve independence. The Philippine Independence Act has already been passed, and in a year, an autonomous government can be organized under the highest commissioner of the United States to test their ability to self-govern. Why is this possible? Of course, credit must be given to the educational policies that the United States has implemented in the Philippines for more than ten years. The situation in elementary schools is like this, and the achievements in secondary schools, vocational schools, and universities are also very good. However, their vocational schools are not yet very developed, so they are now also planning to add more. I visited one or two vocational schools. The agricultural vocational school in Baguio is very large in scale. As for the children of overseas Chinese in the Philippines, they can enter government-established elementary schools for free, just like the natives. Some overseas Chinese feel that if this continues, the children of overseas Chinese may forget their motherland, so everyone has risen up to find a way to run their own elementary schools and also have several secondary schools. In the past, these schools were scattered and inconsistent. Later, everyone united to organize an Overseas Chinese Education Association to manage the secondary and elementary schools run by overseas Chinese. In the past, the funding for each school was first raised through private donations. Since the establishment of the Overseas Chinese Education Association, it has been decided to collect 3% of the business tax of overseas Chinese merchants as an educational surcharge for funding, so the overseas Chinese schools can be maintained. In the past, the educational surcharge was the highest around 1923, with an annual collection of as much as 120,000 yuan. Now, because the market is sluggish, the annual income is less than 20,000 yuan, which is difficult to maintain, so special donations are being solicited and educational lottery tickets are being issued, which shows the economic difficulty. Because the weather is too hot, public elementary schools in the Philippines do not have classes in the afternoon; they only study for half a day each day, and Saturdays are also holidays. There are only five half-day classes a week. Overseas Chinese elementary schools have classes all day long. Not only all day long, but also divided into two shifts. In the morning, they study Chinese; in the afternoon, they study English. They must study English from the second semester of the second grade. The Chinese and English class schedules are not uniform. Graduation is also divided into two types. Diplomas are issued for both Chinese and English graduation, similar to the methods of church schools in China in the past. With this method, the small children have to study two languages every day in very hot weather, which is certainly very hard. Moreover, the Chinese curriculum follows the domestic curriculum standards, and the English follows the Philippine public elementary school standards, which is even more difficult. Overseas Chinese are preparing to have their children graduate in English and then enter Philippine public secondary schools. After graduating in Chinese, they can enter overseas Chinese secondary schools or return to China to enter mainland secondary schools. What will be the result? Because the amount of curriculum is too heavy, often both languages are not learned well. In addition, there is another drawback, which is the repetition of courses. For example, arithmetic is a subject in the Chinese curriculum, and it is also a subject in the English curriculum. Isn't this wasting energy? This situation must be reformed. I have contributed some suggestions for improvement to them; I don't know if they will be adopted in the future. One very good achievement of overseas Chinese schools is that the elementary school students in each school can speak Mandarin. Eighty percent of the overseas Chinese in the Philippines are from Xiamen, and 20% are from Guangdong. In the past, overseas Chinese spoke their local dialects or English. Older overseas Chinese spoke Spanish, and the languages were very different. Now it's good. As long as you speak standard Mandarin, most students can understand it. How do they teach? Their teachers all use Mandarin to teach, and they also use the Xiamen dialect for comparison, so students have to remember two pronunciations for one word. Although it is a bit painful when learning, elementary school students can recognize Mandarin, at least they can understand Mandarin. This way, when we Chinese meet, we don't have to speak in English; we can exchange opinions with each other in Mandarin. This is a big improvement, and credit must be given to Mandarin education. Perhaps the situation in China is not as good as in Southeast Asian islands. In Shanghai, not every teacher who teaches Mandarin can use standard Mandarin to teach, which really needs to be improved," he said. Universal Education Movement to be Implemented in this City Starting in July 300 Schools to be Established Each Year Survey Work to be Completed Next Month According to statistics from the Shanghai Education Bureau, the number of illiterate people in Shanghai, excluding the special zone, is about 550,000 adults and about 150,000 children (excluding students), totaling over 750,000 people. In order to eliminate illiteracy and popularize education throughout the city, the local educational authorities have decided to first launch a literacy education campaign. A reporter from the Shanghai Times specifically interviewed Mr. Jiang Jianbai, Chief of the Fourth Section of the Education Bureau. Mr. Jiang said: "The survey will be completed next month. To promote universal education, the first step is to conduct a survey of the number of illiterate people in the city. The survey forms are designed by the Education Bureau and conducted by the Public Security Bureau. It is expected that this work will be fully completed by next month at the latest. Currently, various implementation matters are being designed and prepared. The implementation period for the literacy education campaign will begin in July, which will be completed by the end of June. Six sessions will be held each year. The implementation method is to divide the year into six sessions, each lasting two months. At least 300 schools will be established each session, with one teacher per school, teaching for six hours a day, divided into three shifts: morning, afternoon, and evening. It is estimated that there will be 50 students per class. With six sessions a year, a total of 540,000 people can be reached. Teaching materials will be selected by the Bureau. The "Shanghai Citizen Literacy Textbook" will only include 600 commonly used characters due to the short time of two months. The content will be divided into New Life, Citizen, Hygiene, and Nature, with both text and illustrations. This book will be published by the 15th of next month. The budget for the above work is 200,000 yuan. Literacy requires practical application. The Bureau also believes that after literacy, it is even more important to be able to use literacy. Literacy is an important task for popularizing education, but the meaning of literacy (i.e., civic education) is equally important. Therefore, the Education Bureau will launch very popular publications and will also unite with local social education institutions, enthusiastic individuals, and cultural groups to jointly promote and implement this."
