Local Supplement of Shen Bao, Special Film Edition

The Salaries of Two Hollywood Child Stars, Jackie Cooper and Shirley Temple (Part 2) by Ti Yun

Paramount was the first major company to hire Shirley Temple on a monthly basis. Initially, Shirley was filming two-reel short films for Educational Pictures, earning only ten dollars a day. Paramount was looking for inexpensive, ordinary child actors, and Shirley Temple auditioned along with many other children. Paramount immediately hired her at a salary of one hundred dollars per week. However, after the film was completed, Paramount did not renew her contract, even though the film performed exceptionally well, which everyone acknowledged. As a result, Shirley Temple had to return to making short films. This was Paramount's first major misstep.

Some time later, Fox hired Shirley Temple to film "Stand Up and Cheer," with a salary of one hundred and fifty dollars per week. While filming this picture, they signed her current seven-year long-term contract. However, Shirley's meteoric rise was not due to Fox's efforts. Shirley's stardom should still be attributed to Paramount because "Little Miss Marker," which she filmed for Paramount, established her status.

"Little Miss Marker" earned Paramount millions of dollars, but the total amount they paid Shirley was only one thousand and fifty dollars, which was one hundred and fifty dollars per week for a total of seven weeks. There is also an interesting story. The famous comedian, Adolphe Menjou, while collaborating with Shirley Temple on "Little Miss Marker," had a whimsical idea. He discussed with the company management, offering to forgo his usual forty thousand dollars per film fee and instead take a small percentage of the film's profits. The company agreed, thinking Adolphe Menjou would regret it. Unexpectedly, "Little Miss Marker" was a huge success, and Adolphe Menjou also made a small fortune. Although Paramount made a large profit from Shirley, they did not keep her, still allowing her to return to Fox. This was Paramount's second major misstep.

After Shirley returned to Fox, the Fox authorities still only gave her one hundred and fifty dollars per week and did not sign a long-term contract with her. This can also be considered an oversight on the part of the Fox authorities. It wasn't until Shirley finished filming "Baby Take a Bow" that Fox realized their mistake. Fortunately, Fox's manager, Winfield Sheehan, took early measures to remedy the situation, and this shining pearl was not snatched away by others, which can be said to be a great stroke of luck for Fox.

But even more absurd and perplexing, after Shirley finished filming "Baby Take a Bow" and had already become famous, Sheehan actually agreed to lend this cash cow to Paramount to film "Now and Forever." Fox received only three thousand five hundred dollars in compensation, while Shirley received only the same one hundred and fifty dollars as before, and Paramount still hadn't thought about signing a contract with her. This can be said to be Paramount's third major blunder and absurdity.

At this point, Shirley's parents gradually realized that they had been too foolish, allowing the company to earn millions in profits while they continued to receive a small salary of one hundred and fifty dollars per week. They began to protest. At the same time, a group of Hollywood agents knew that this was a "rare commodity" and eagerly contacted Temple's parents, wanting to become Shirley's agent. According to the usual rules, an agent's commission is ten percent of the star's salary. However, these agents all waived Shirley Temple's commission, just wanting to be her agent. One agent even offered a bonus of twenty thousand dollars in addition to forgoing the commission. What was the reason for this?

It turned out that they also had ulterior motives. They knew that Shirley was a "rare commodity," and they thought that if they could find a way to get her, they could "manipulate the market" and use Shirley's contract, along with other people's contracts, to blackmail the film companies. Even if they didn't make money from Shirley herself, they could make a huge profit elsewhere. This was their evil plan.

At this time, Sheehan realized that the situation had become critical and had to use his skills. Without anyone knowing, he brought the Temple couple to the company. He said to them, "Why hire an agent and let others make money for nothing? I understand Shirley's value. I am willing to handle things fairly and guarantee that you won't be at a disadvantage. I will give Shirley one thousand two hundred and fifty dollars per week and also give Mrs. Temple two hundred and fifty dollars per week. What do you think?" He had a friendly expression on his face, with a sincere spirit in his eyes. This made the Temple couple agree without hesitation. Sheehan immediately tore up the one hundred and fifty dollar contract in front of them and signed a new seven-year contract.

The total salary for seven years was four hundred and fifty-five thousand dollars, which was a considerable sum. But if Mr. or Mrs. Temple had insisted a little more, they would have gotten even more. (The End)

Movie Review: "Poor and Happy" by Ji Han 95

The lead actor in this film, Liu Yalis, was the protagonist of the famous film "All Quiet on the Western Front." Naturally, people are very concerned about him. However, a relatively successful and promising actor is often brutally ruined in vulgar films. He is so stiff and devoid of emotion in "Poor and Happy," even exhibiting a lack of intelligence, which is a perfect example.

It's not that Liu Yalis can't act, but in vulgar stories, he cannot develop his talents. The problem lies in the playwright's excessive commercialism and lack of creative ability. Of course, we cannot ignore that "Poor and Happy" lacks a relatively serious theme. Even if we settle for the so-called entertainment value, it does not achieve much because the cliché script and far-fetched plot determine its low artistic value.

Relatively speaking, the stage song and dance and the sword fight are more watchable. The former, with its decadent music, represents the splendor and brilliance of capitalist film form, while the latter, with its resonant sound of swords, also gives people romantic fantasies. From this perspective, the director of the song and dance scenes has made some contributions.

Furthermore, perhaps people feel some goodwill towards Peggy Feaas, who plays the singer Gai Bi. Indeed, she is somewhat pleasing to people. Her slender figure and charming posture, although she cannot give people a more sincere emotion, she does not overly disappoint people. In addition, the one who plays the guide, Tang Ke, also has a relatively consistent personality expression. This is due to his constant removal of his shoes to depict his laziness and casualness, which can give the audience a clear concept in the movie and is a good method.

But what else does it give us here? A group of young men, in order to win the favor of a singer, use the excuse of returning a garter to make a young man who has never been near a woman make many jokes. At the same time, he and another girl fall in love for real, and that's all.

My View on Tolstoy's "Resurrection" by William 96

"Resurrection" is the representative work of the Russian writer Tolstoy's life, and it is also the dividing line between his early and late works after the dramatic change in Tolstoy's thoughts and personality. Since the advent of "Resurrection," the silent atmosphere in the literary world has been shaken up all over the world.

Tolstoy's works mostly depict the real situation of objective life, and explain it without distorting the entity in his ideals. Even the personality of the secondary important characters in his works is very well grasped. Each character is vividly written under Tolstoy's pen, making the relationship between the plot and the characteristics of the characters more closely linked. However, Tolstoy never deviates from the original track due to the words in his pen and the feelings in his heart.

Before Tolstoy wrote "Resurrection," he himself had thought that this should be his last literary work in his life. Therefore, Tolstoy was determined to fully express the ambitions he had accumulated in his heart, and give them a serious criticism or instruction separately. For example, the issue of men and women, the issue of land reform, the issue of prison reform... "Resurrection" has detailed discussions on all major issues in Tsarist Russian society and religion at that time. In this way, in terms of writing "Resurrection," Tolstoy still adheres to the unified rules of literature, and collects very rich materials on politics and religion.

The main theme of "Resurrection" is what Tolstoy often loved in his life. In Tolstoy's novels, it can often be found that the souls of several kinds of people have undergone a period of torture, and then they have an epiphany. In "Resurrection," he portrays a selfish nobleman and a fallen prostitute, whose souls are suddenly saved and reborn. Tolstoy's purpose in writing "Resurrection" was to use economic power to save persecuted Christians and to show how a reformed soul could be saved.

This is the third time that "Resurrection" has been made into a film art work. Its literary evaluation has been described above. Its value in film art should be very high. Because this work not only relies on the richness of the original content to give it great assistance, but also achieves the highest success in the skills of film art. The director's expression of the author's spirit is able to faithfully maintain it. The mysterious atmosphere of the original work is also handled very appropriately, which is the most important point of "Resurrection."

The male protagonist here is a young man from Moscow. He is full of utopian new ideas, he is a believer in socialism, and he is also a legal authority. When he finds a peasant woman on trial in court, who is his former lover, at this time, his passion is burning in his heart, and he can't help but give up his property and family and go to Siberia with the peasant woman. This is how Tolstoy has this new idea of expressing the love between a couple.

The director, Mamulin, can grasp the charm of Tolstoy's original work, and the use of rich experience, organic techniques, and the victory of actor distribution are all unique features of this film. Unfortunately, in some scenes, the director could not grasp the center of gravity of the drama, which made the performance a little scattered.

Celebrating the Glory of National Films, Jincheng Re-screens "Song of the Fishermen" by Fang 97

At this Soviet Russian international film exhibition, film circles in Europe and the United States have all selected films to participate. The central party and government authorities have also selected several national famous films to go to the exhibition. Now news has come that "Song of the Fishermen," which was continuously screened for eighty-four days at the Jincheng Grand Theater, has won an honorary award. This time, Chinese films can be praised by foreigners and win a place in the international film scene. It must be said to be the glory of the entire domestic film industry, and it is also the beginning of Chinese films moving towards the world. The Jincheng Grand Theater has always been aimed at promoting domestic films. Now, in order to celebrate the glory of domestic films, it plans to re-screen "Song of the Fishermen" for a few days after "The She-Serpent," so that a group of friends who have not seen this film and want to see it again have the opportunity to appreciate it.

Film Novel: The Iron Duke (6) by Xin Zhi 99

Wellington said: "The shock I felt was really too great. You don't know, although I have never met you, I already know everything about you..."

Chichester coughed and said: "The Duchess of Richmond said that your husband will be back in London next week."

Frances said: "That's right. I have to go back to see him. He is not raising funds here."

Wellington said: "He knew you came here."

Frances said: "I thought I wouldn't tell him."

Wellington again asked: "Then why did you come here after all?"

Frances simply said: "To see you. Just to see you, in this place, at this time, just like now. They say Napoleon is in Quatre Bras not far from here. Is there any danger here?"

Wellington said: "There is no great danger, you don't have to be afraid."

Frances said: "I am not afraid. I even hope you say there is danger. I like dangerous things."

Outside the Duchess of Richmond's mansion, a messenger suddenly galloped from the darkness. The guards outside the mansion immediately stepped forward to stop him. But the man on horseback threw a letter on the ground and shouted: "General Blücher's urgent report, take it in quickly!" As he said that, he turned his horse around and galloped away. The guard examined the letter and hurriedly entered the hall and handed it to an officer, who immediately gave it to Wellington. He opened it and his face turned pale. He left Frances and walked out of the small house. A secretary greeted him. Wellington whispered: "Napoleon's army is coming here soon. He ambushed Quatre Bras, and Blücher was unprepared. Now the national army has collapsed."

Ten minutes later, the officers in the ballroom had quietly dispersed. They were orderly and did not appear flustered. At this time, troops on the street were entering in batches. In the dark night, the sound of horns echoed each other, feeling particularly desolate. Wellington's officers also took over in shifts one by one. By dawn, Wellington's army had arrived at Waterloo. After twenty-four hours of hand-to-hand combat, bloodshed, slaughter, and death, when the two armies met, both sides were led by military geniuses, and they were evenly matched, making it difficult to distinguish the winner. At first, the French army had the upper hand. Blücher's reinforcements had not yet arrived. But by night, the Germans had arrived.

The tragedy of killing and death was even more severe towards the end. After the German army reorganized its forces, it blocked the last desperate battle of Napoleon's Imperial Army. These French troops, veterans of hundreds of battles, shouted the name of Napoleon, and died one by one, exhausted. When this battle cloud blew past, Napoleon's army was in ruins, leaving only a few incomplete soldiers, stumbling and fleeing into the darkness, leaving behind corpses of men and horses, scattered and messy, with no one to care for them.

But the defeat of one army is the victory of another army, although the price of victory is exchanged for countless heads and hot blood. The corpses on the battlefield were piled up like mountains, and their blood seeped into the land. Among those people, many were dancing gracefully in Mrs. Richmond's mansion a few days ago, and now they have all become white bones on the banks of the Wu Ding River. This is the cruel price of victory and glory. In a broken village house, Wellington set up his headquarters. He read the list of dead soldiers, and he couldn't help but lower his head in grief. (To be continued)

Wuxi Hunan Refugees Loot in Broad Daylight 100

Yesterday at approximately 9:00 AM, over a hundred Hunan refugees suddenly arrived at the Hua Da Fang Zhuang area in the Third District and forcibly demanded rice and grain from the local residents. They also arbitrarily harassed and looted property in the Hui Wan Li area. It is estimated that a local villager, Hui Tang, lost over 130 yuan in cash, as well as pearls and clothing worth about 300-400 yuan. The 8th Sub-Bureau of Public Safety, upon receiving the report, immediately dispatched police to suppress the unrest. Additionally, around 200 refugees arrived in the Hui Shan area. The Public Safety Bureau dispatched police to escort them out of the area.

Third Phase of Baojia System Work Begins 101

The First District Office, in order to actively carry out the third phase of Baojia system work, specially convened a joint meeting of various township chiefs and representatives from educational institutions. The meeting was chaired by Qian Zhongliang. The following resolutions were passed: 1. Divide all townships in the district into five major groups, with each group consisting of four to five townships. Each township will form a small group, with the township chief serving as the director of the small group, responsible for guiding and supervising the completion of the work. Specific methods for educational personnel to assist have been separately formulated and will be distributed by the district for application. 2. Within each major group, the group leader, together with the township Baojia chiefs and educational personnel from each small group, will conduct practical investigations of ten households within the scope of each Bao. Any doubts will be clarified by the major group leader. 3. Each major group can hold meetings on different days. Schools can suspend classes for a maximum of three days to assist with household investigations, and the district office will notify the Public Safety Bureau to provide assistance at any time.

Adultery Leads to Murder of Woman 102

Qian Jianjie, a doctor of osteology in Yangshu Yi Li, Tenth District, was well-off. After being widowed several years ago, he married Ge A Huan's daughter, Yu Ying, from nearby Renli Bridge as his second wife. Yu Ying, currently 22 years old, is beautiful. The couple had a very affectionate relationship. However, recently, Yu Ying became intimately involved with her cousin, Wang Mingting. Jianjie had heard rumors of this, so on the 2nd of this month, he pretended to have business in the city and left home. Yu Ying, believing this to be true, then made an appointment with Mingting to meet secretly at home in the afternoon. Around 4:00 PM, Jianjie suddenly returned home. Mingting was unable to escape in time and hid under the bed in the back building. This was discovered by Jianjie, who angrily beat Mingting. Mingting was seriously injured and escaped. On the evening of the same day around 9:00 PM, Yu Ying, feeling ashamed and indignant, committed suicide by hanging herself at her parents' home. A Huan hastily prepared her for burial.

Changzhou Urgent Telegram to Stop the New Regulations on House Tax 103

On the 10th, the Wu Yi County Chamber of Commerce convened a joint meeting of its executive and supervisory committees to discuss the new regulations on the Jiangsu provincial house tax. The tax rates have been changed significantly, and the levy extends to residential housing, which is beyond the capacity of the people to bear. It was resolved to send separate telegrams to the central and provincial governments, as well as the Jiangsu Donation and Tax Supervision Committee, requesting a halt to the implementation of the regulations to alleviate the people's hardship. It was also proposed that the Business Tax Bureau periodically begin re-examining account books. At a time of extreme financial strain and industrial and commercial decline, with business scope shrinking year after year and business conditions this spring being sluggish, it seems difficult to use last year's account books as a standard. It is proposed that the Business Tax Bureau consider the current state of commerce and reduce tax amounts to alleviate the difficulties of Jiangsu merchants. It was resolved to publicly select representatives to go to the Business Tax Bureau to present the difficult situation of commerce and request a reduction in tax amounts.

Chongming Third District Inspector Strictly Prohibits Opium and Gambling 104

Since Zhou Dingchang resigned as the inspector of the Third Sub-Bureau of Chongming's Third District, Nie Xifan has been appointed to fill the position. It is said that Nie is honest, upright, diligent, and responsible. Every day, he personally supervises the police to clean the streets, regulate road rules, strictly prohibit opium and gambling, and pay attention to local security, striving to eliminate past malpractices. Therefore, the people of the entire district deeply rejoice at having found the right person.

Changshu Opening Coffin for Autopsy in East Zhou Murder Case 105

Chen Bingfu, a resident of Wanfu Bridge in Dongzhou City, Sixth District, was excessively spoiled by his parents in his youth. He squandered his family property on opium and gambling. His mother, Sun, hated him to the bone. His younger brother, Wu Bao, inherited his uncle's property and lived in a new house in Haicheng. Unfortunately, he died young. His brother's wife, Xia, remarried to Chen Xiaoguai. At that time, Bingfu wanted to sell the new house. Xia contacted his aunt Sun, and the mother and son split the price of the house equally. Xiaoguai and Xia officially moved into the new house and lived with Sun, as if they were mother and son. On the third day of the first month of this lunar year, Bingfu returned home, intending to pay the difference for the house. The next day, news suddenly spread that Bingfu had hanged himself. As a result, rumors spread, some saying he was beaten to death, others saying he was strangled. The truth remains unclear. Currently, the county government has detained all relevant personnel. It is scheduled to open the coffin for autopsy at Zha Ba Wan outside the North Gate on the 11th of this month to clarify the truth. The coffin has already been transported to the city in advance.

Yin Jiang Quarrel Over Debt Leads to Murder 106

In the Yangku Hengjing Shao area of the Fourth District, a woman named Zhang Lu, aged about fifty, had been a widow for many years. Her son, Caisheng, worked as a farmer. Last spring, he and a villager, Xu Zhicheng, jointly purchased an ox for 72 yuan. Zhang Lu paid 18 yuan. After the drought last summer, the Zhang family experienced financial difficulties and sold their share of the ox to the Xu family, agreeing that the previous price and costs for soybean cakes would amount to 25.2 yuan, which had not yet been repaid. On the 8th, Zhang Lu demanded the money from the Xu family but was unsuccessful. She quarreled with Zhicheng and his son, Jialiang. Jialiang punched Zhang in the nose, causing her to bleed profusely and die. Her son then reported to the township chief, Ye Hengxi, who detained the two perpetrators, father and son, and reported to the district office and then by telephone to the county government. On the morning of the 9th, an investigator named Jiang Cheng was dispatched to the village to examine the body. It was confirmed that she died from suffocation due to the injury. The two perpetrators were taken to the city for interrogation.

Local Organizations Request Suspension of House Tax 107

The Ministry of Finance submitted a proposal to the provincial government to collect house tax from various counties. The chambers of commerce of Su, Xi, and Yi counties have protested, urgently requesting a suspension of the tax. The chambers of commerce and other organizations in this county also believe that since the shop house tax in Jiangsu province has not yet been reduced or exempted, it is inappropriate to levy tax on people's own homes, which would be equivalent to the province taking ownership of the people's houses and making them pay rent every month. Moreover, after the disasters in Jiangsu province, farmers are bankrupt and commerce is declining. Our government should be trying to salvage the situation and rescue the people from their plight. How can it exploit them to the fullest extent and increase their burden by forcing them to pay house tax monthly? It is no wonder that the people are collectively clamoring and opposing the tax. Self-occupied houses are different from shops and have no profit-making nature. What is the justification for forcibly levying the tax? As for public security expenses, Jiangyin already has a corner-of-the-mouth donation of one jiao per mu [a Chinese unit of area] for the expenses, which already heavily burdens the people. The county's police expenses have a budgeted amount that is sufficient to cover the costs. If there is a need for a reorganization plan, it is only necessary to unify income and expenditure to eliminate waste, and it is not appropriate to impose additional taxes, which would cause further disturbances. Because the matter involves increasing the people's burden, a telegram was sent yesterday (the 9th) to the ministry, council, and provincial government, requesting a suspension of the implementation to comfort the people.

The following directors attended the Sino-British Board yesterday: Sir Meyricke, Li Shu Hua, Soong Tsung-liang, Tseng Yung-fu, Yeh Kung-chao, Chen Chi-cai, M. Blondeel, Jing En, and A. H. F. Special Committee of the Local Association Decides to Implement Relief Plan 113

Government and Silver Firms Provide Small Credit Loans; Chambers of Commerce and Other Groups to Hold Joint Meeting; Party and Government to be Called Together by Mayor Wu to Study

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, with regard to the issue of relieving the market, the party, government, and business circles are conducting separate studies. The special committee of the local association has made considerable decisions on the relief plan. The City Chamber of Commerce and other groups will hold a joint meeting to petition Minister Kong for adoption. The details are as follows:

Party, Government, and Business Circles to Conduct Separate Studies

Since Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi convened various sectors to discuss relief measures, it has been decided to adhere to the principle of automatic relief and conduct separate studies by all parties. The party and government will jointly hold a meeting convened by Mayor Wu, which will include the Bureau of Social Affairs and the Bureau of Finance. Although the date of the meeting has not been announced, it is certain that it will be held within the next day or two. On the yarn industry side, Guo Shun, the representative of the Wing On Textile Mill, is responsible for convening the meeting. According to Mr. Guo, who spoke to the Xin Sheng News Agency reporter yesterday morning, they have decided to hold a meeting today to discuss the matter, but the location will not be publicly announced.

Decisions to be Submitted to Kong for Adoption

The local association, after the special committee meeting to study the relief plan for industry and commerce, has made considerable decisions. Regarding the 5 million yuan small credit loan case, it is proposed that the government and silver firms each contribute 2.5 million yuan to organize an agency to handle it, with the Chamber of Commerce and the local association responsible for the review. It is said that this decision will be submitted to Minister Kong for adoption.

Local Association Responds to Inquiry

The local association responded to the inquiry yesterday, saying: "Respectfully replying, upon receiving your letter, which stated that industry and commerce in this port urgently need relief and proposed two force options, requesting a collective discussion, we convened a special committee meeting on the 9th to first discuss the first option, namely the small credit loan method for industry and commerce. We collectively advocated that silver firms initiate the organization of a syndicate with a total amount of 5 million yuan, specifically for small loans to industry and commerce. At the same time, the Chamber of Commerce and the local association will jointly petition the Ministry of Finance to appropriate funds as appropriate. As for all loan procedures, they will be approved by the syndicate, etc. We are still waiting for the City Chamber of Commerce, the Bankers' Association, and the Silver Firms Association to separately resolve the implementation. In addition to separate letters, we hereby reply in advance. We hope you will take note."

Scheduled for Another Joint Meeting

The Local Association, the City Chamber of Commerce, the Bankers' Association, the Silver Firms Association, and other four organizations are scheduled to convene a joint meeting within a few days to further study the relief plan for implementation. In addition, the Silver Firms Association and the Bankers' Association will also convene separate meetings to discuss the small loan issue within the relief plan for implementation.

Kong Expresses Scheduled Continuation of Discussion

The Xin Sheng News Agency reporter visited Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi yesterday morning to inquire about the issue of relieving the market. Mr. Kong said that the issue is not so simple that it can be described in words, but he has now ordered the party, government, and business circles to separately study the methods in detail. After receiving the reports from the various related parties, he will schedule a meeting to continue discussing everything.

Silver Market Call Loans Slightly Easier

The silver market call loans opened for several days have been around 8-9 percent. According to the Xin Sheng News Agency reporter, although the various silver firms have been making as many loans as possible with goods as collateral for various industries and businesses, they are particularly cautious due to their own problems. Therefore, silver firms do not need to borrow from each other, and call loans remain flat. As for the various industries, due to a lack of purchasing power and the accumulation of inventory, although the credit situation has gradually eased compared to before, it has not fully recovered.

City Federation Requests Reduction of Land Prices 114

Sent Letters to Various Organizations Yesterday Requesting a Unified Stance

The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation, in order to request the Municipal Council to reduce land price assessments to ease the burden on landlords and promote the realization of the rent reduction movement, sent letters to various organizations yesterday requesting a unified stance. The original letter stated: "Respectfully informing you, since the January 28th Shanghai War, all industries have been depressed, and the market has deteriorated daily, without recovery. In recent years, even stores that have been in business for decades and have established credit have been unable to maintain themselves due to the social depression, and have closed down one after another, resulting in some families being bankrupted and others being displaced. Vacant houses in the city are lined up like combs, with no one interested. This situation is truly pitiful. The reason for this is that the land price assessment in this city has been increasing year by year, and the land tax has also increased accordingly. The burden on landlords is several times what it used to be. Property owners build houses, and due to cost considerations, the rent must be high. Therefore, the residents of this city have been running around calling for rent reduction for two years. Although there are some wise people who have voluntarily reduced rent to ease the burden on merchants, they are truly admirable. However, stubborn people treat tenants as slaves and arbitrarily oppress them, ignoring the rent reduction issue altogether, which is truly heartbreaking. In view of this, the Federation believes that addressing the symptoms instead of the root cause will not be effective. This is a clear ancient lesson. The executive committee of the Federation discussed the matter yesterday and resolved that requesting rent reduction is like ladling soup to stop boiling, and it is better to remove the firewood from under the pot first. We propose that the various legal entities in this city unanimously advocate requesting the Municipal Council to reassess the land prices in this city to the lowest possible price to ease the burden on property owners and avoid excuses. If the Municipal Council believes that implementing lower land price assessments will reduce tax revenue and hinder taxation, then please collect house tax on vacant houses in the city on a per-household basis, as the various legal entities in this city have already resolved, to supplement the revenue. This will be more than adequate. On the Municipal Council's side, shifting the collection of taxes seems to have no loss whatsoever. With the land tax reduced, the rent on houses will naturally be reduced accordingly, and merchants will be happy to rent them to avoid the burden. This is clear logic. Merchants can operate with peace of mind, maintain their business, and the past prosperity of this city will not be difficult to restore, etc." It was recorded in the minutes and sent to you accordingly. We request your organization to investigate, hold a meeting as soon as possible, and reply with the details of the resolution. This is addressed to various organizations.
